### Hypothesis: 1
# *from global gold standard* *to gone* *in* <_num_> *years!*
# *from global gold standard* *to gone* *in* <more than _high_> *years!*
# contradiction
# *from global gold standard*: from global gold standard; from just beginning; from sold everywhere; from best in its industry; 
# *to gone*: to gone; to even better; to local loser; to ashes; 
# *in*: in; at; with no; now; 
# *years!*: years!; cycles; seconds; seconds; 

# args:  <<*from global gold standard* = from global gold standard>>  <<*to gone* = to gone>>  <<*in* = in>>  <<*years!* = seconds>>

### Hypothesis: 1
# *from global gold standard* *to gone* *in* <_num_> *years!*
# *from global gold standard* *to gone* *in* <less than _low_> *years!*
# contradiction
# *from global gold standard*: from global gold standard; from just beginning; from sold everywhere; from best in its industry; 
# *to gone*: to gone; to even better; to local loser; to ashes; 
# *in*: in; at; with no; now; 
# *years!*: years!; cycles; seconds; seconds;
